SENTIENT SPECIES:
Slim Antoids: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have bilateral symmetry and a slim shape. They are gregarious and have a complex system of social rules. They first evolved on Hylon VI in 347.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: -1 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: 1
Flying Ursoids: Always at war with someone, or everyone, or one another. They have bilateral symmetry. They can fly. They are gregarious and have a complex system of social castes. They first evolved on Cykov I in 314.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: -1 INT: 0 CHA: -1
Telepathic Grey Deep Dwellers: They live in the deep oceans or in deep caves, hiding. Their presence can go unnoticed for a long time. They have grey skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are fond of practical jokes and value personal integrity above all else. They first evolved on Genur VI in 327.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 0 CON: -1 INT: 1 CHA: -1
Telepathic Antoids: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have bilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are fond of practical jokes and unwilling to compromise. They first evolved on Erebus V in 350.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 1 CON: -1 INT: 1 CHA: 1
Red Dwarfoids with Threefold Symmetry: Fond of drink and industry - especially building strange contraptions. They have red skin. They have trilateral symmetry. They are violent and believe that each individual must serve the community. They first evolved on Cykov I in 281.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 0 CON: 2 INT: 1 CHA: -1
Telepathic Grey Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have grey skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are cowardly and deeply rationalist. They were created by the Church of Six-Legged Ursoids on Sativex III as servants in 375.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: 1 INT: -1 CHA: -1
Four-Armed Grey Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have grey skin. They have four arms. They have bilateral symmetry. They are meditative and believe that each individual must serve the community. They were created by the Empire of Slim Antoids on Golet I as servants in 389.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 1 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 0
Immortal Orange Antoids: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have orange skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They have no fixed lifespan and only die of disease or accidents. They are gregarious and have a complex system of social rules. They first evolved on Hylon VI in 302.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 0
Four-Armed Dwarfoids with Five-fold Symmetry: Fond of drink and industry - especially building strange contraptions. They have four arms. They have five-fold symmetry. They are violent and value personal integrity above all else. They first evolved on Sativex III in 329.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 1 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: -2
Feathered Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have bilateral symmetry. They are modest and have a deep need to conform. They were created by the Empire of Slim Antoids on Genur VI as servants in 405.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 1 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: -1

CIVILISATIONS:
THE EMPIRE OF SLIM ANTOIDS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Empire of 17 planets, with 454 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
22 billion Slim Antoids.
32 billion enslaved Flying Ursoids.
38 billion enslaved Telepathic Grey Deep Dwellers.
132 billion enslaved Telepathic Antoids.
32 billion enslaved Red Dwarfoids with Threefold Symmetry.
4 billion enslaved Telepathic Grey Robots.
6 billion enslaved Four-Armed Grey Robots.
140 billion enslaved Immortal Orange Antoids.
39 billion enslaved Four-Armed Dwarfoids with Five-fold Symmetry.
9 billion enslaved Feathered Robots.
It controls a Master Computer.
It controls a Virtual Reality Matrix.

	Their Stats are: STR: -3 DEX: -2 CON: 0 INT: -4 CHA: -2
PLANETS:
EREBUS V
A life-bearing planet of the Empire of Slim Antoids.
It is somewhat polluted.
It is populated by:
11 billion enslaved Telepathic Antoids

A vast museum, built by the Empire of Slim Antoids in 410
A repair bay, built by the Empire of Slim Antoids in 423
Beaufiful Aurorae: The solar wind makes bright displays of flickering green at the planet's poles.
Lifeforms of note:
Shape-shifters: A predatory creature able to mimic any other, even a sentient one.
Radiovores: These small worm-like creatures derive their energy directly from exposed deposits of radioactive materials.
Gas bags: Held aloft by sacs of hydrogen, these delicate creatures float about everywhere.

The ruins of a military base, built by the Church of Six-Legged Ursoids in 388, destroyed in 391 during the collapse of the Church of Six-Legged Ursoids.
The ruins of a military base, built by the Church of Six-Legged Ursoids in 310, destroyed in 387 due to orbital bombardment by the Church of Six-Legged Ursoids.

The ruins of a military base, built by the Second Empire of Four-Armed White Catoids in 85, destroyed in 109 due to orbital bombardment by the Republic of Antoids, Robots, Dwarfoids and Catoids.
